hagia_sophia = {
	start = 151
	date = 537.01.01
	time = { months = 0	}
	build_cost = 0
	can_be_moved = no
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 10
	starting_tier = 2
	type = monument

	build_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = orthodox
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = apostolic
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = syriac
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = nestorian
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = coptic
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion_group = muslim
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = catholic
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
		}
	}

	on_built = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = hagia_sophia_now_mosque
			}
			show_ambient_object = hagia_sophia_minarets
		}
		else = {
			show_ambient_object = hagia_sophia
		}
	}

	on_destroyed = {
		hide_ambient_object = hagia_sophia_minarets
		hide_ambient_object = hagia_sophia
	}

	can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = orthodox
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = apostolic
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = syriac
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = nestorian
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = coptic
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND= {
				religion_group = muslim
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = catholic
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
		}
	}

	can_upgrade_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = orthodox
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = apostolic
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = syriac
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = nestorian
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = coptic
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND= {
				religion_group = muslim
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = catholic
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
		}
	}

	keep_trigger = {
	}

	tier_0 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 0
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 0
		}
		province_modifiers = {
		}
		area_modifier = {
		}
		country_modifiers = {
		}
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_1 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 120
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		province_modifiers = {
		}
		area_modifier = {
		}
		country_modifiers = {
			tolerance_own = 0.25
			tolerance_heretic = 0.25
		}
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_2 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 240
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 2500
		}
		province_modifiers = {
		}
		area_modifier = {
		}
		country_modifiers = {
			tolerance_own = 0.5
			tolerance_heretic = 0.5
			monthly_piety = 0.001
			yearly_patriarch_authority = 0.002
			papal_influence = 0.5
			church_loyalty_modifier = 0.05
		}
		on_upgraded = {
			owner = {
				add_estate_loyalty = {
					estate = estate_church
					loyalty = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}

	tier_3 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 480
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 5000
		}
		province_modifiers = {
		}
		area_modifier = {
		}
		country_modifiers = {
			tolerance_own = 1
			tolerance_heretic = 1
			monthly_piety = 0.002
			yearly_patriarch_authority = 0.005
			papal_influence = 1
			church_loyalty_modifier = 0.1
		}
		on_upgraded = {
			owner = {
				add_estate_loyalty = {
					estate = estate_church
					loyalty = 10
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

stonehenge = {
	start = 10357
	date = -2500.01.01
	time = { months = 0 }
	build_cost = 0
	can_be_moved = yes
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 2
	starting_tier = 0
	type = monument

	build_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion_group = pagan
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				culture = english
				OR = {
					has_owner_culture = yes
					has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	on_built = {
		show_ambient_object = stonehenge
	}

	on_destroyed = {
		hide_ambient_object = stonehenge
	}

	can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion_group = pagan
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				culture = english
				OR = {
					has_owner_culture = yes
					has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	can_upgrade_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion_group = pagan
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				culture = english
				OR = {
					has_owner_culture = yes
					has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	keep_trigger = {
	}

	tier_0 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 0
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 0
		}
		province_modifiers = {
		}
		area_modifier = {
		}
		country_modifiers = {
		}
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_1 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 120
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		province_modifiers = {
		}
		area_modifier = {
		}
		country_modifiers = {
			tolerance_heretic = 0.5
			tolerance_heathen = 0.5
		}


		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_2 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 240
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 2500
		}
		province_modifiers = {
		}
		area_modifier = {
		}
		country_modifiers = {
			tolerance_heretic = 0.5
			tolerance_heathen = 0.5
			stability_cost_modifier = -0.1
		}
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_3 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 480
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 5000
		}
		province_modifiers = {
		}
		area_modifier = {
		}
		country_modifiers = {
			tolerance_heretic = 1
			tolerance_heathen = 1
			stability_cost_modifier = -0.25
			global_missionary_strength = 0.01
		}
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}
}

buddha_statues = {
	start = 9455
	date = 570.01.01
	time = { months = 0 }
	build_cost = 0
	can_be_moved = yes
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 1
	starting_tier = 1
	type = monument

	build_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = buddhism
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = vajrayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND= {
				religion = mahayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = hinduism
				has_owner_religion = yes
				owner = {
					has_personal_deity = buddha
				}
			}
			AND = {
				religion = shamanism
				has_owner_religion = yes
				owner = {
					has_unlocked_cult = buddhism_cult
				}
			}
		}
	}

	on_built = {
		show_ambient_object = buddha_small
		show_ambient_object = buddha_big
	}

	on_destroyed = {
		hide_ambient_object = buddha_small
		hide_ambient_object = buddha_big
	}

	can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = buddhism
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = vajrayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND= {
				religion = mahayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = hinduism
				has_owner_religion = yes
				owner = {
					has_personal_deity = buddha
				}
			}
			AND = {
				religion = shamanism
				has_owner_religion = yes
				owner = {
					has_unlocked_cult = buddhism_cult
				}
			}
		}
	}

	can_upgrade_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = buddhism

			}
			AND = {
				religion = vajrayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}

				religion = shamanism

parthenon = {
	start = 146
	date = -432.01.01
	time = {
		months = 0
	}
	build_cost = 0
	can_be_moved = no
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 6
	starting_tier = 0
	type = monument

	build_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = pantheon_worship
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				culture_group = byzantine_g
				OR = {
					has_owner_culture = yes
					has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
				}
			}
			AND = {
				religion_group = muslim
				has_owner_religion = yes
				has_global_flag = parthenon_now_mosque
			}
		}
	}

	on_built = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = parthenon_now_mosque
			}
			show_ambient_object = parthenon_minaret
		}
		else = {
			show_ambient_object = parthenon
		}
	}

	on_destroyed = {
		hide_ambient_object = parthenon_minaret
		hide_ambient_object = parthenon
	}

	can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = pantheon_worship
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				culture_group = byzantine_g
				OR = {
					has_owner_culture = yes
					has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
				}
			}
			AND = {
				religion_group = muslim
				has_owner_religion = yes
				has_global_flag = parthenon_now_mosque
			}
		}
	}

	can_upgrade_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = pantheon_worship
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				culture_group = byzantine_g
				OR = {
					has_owner_culture = yes
					has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
				}
			}
			AND = {
				religion_group = muslim

		}

	keep_trigger = {
	}

	tier_0 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 0

		}

		}
	}

	tier_1 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 120
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		province_modifiers = {
		}
		area_modifier = {
			local_unrest = -1
		}
		country_modifiers = {
			advisor_cost = -0.05
		}
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_2 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 240
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 2500
		}
		province_modifiers = {
		}
		area_modifier = {
			local_unrest = -2
		}

			advisor_cost = -0.1
		}
		on_upgraded = {

	tier_3 = {

##### SPECIAL STRAIT PROJECTS #####

palk_strait = {
	start = 6929
	date = 1480.1.1
	time = { months = 0 }
	build_cost = 0
	can_be_moved = no
	starting_tier = 1
	type = canal

	build_trigger = {
		has_global_flag = palk_strait_cyclone_happened
	}

	on_built = {
		add_canal = palk_strait
	}

	on_destroyed = {
		remove_canal = palk_strait
	}

	can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
		has_global_flag = palk_strait_cyclone_happened
	}

	can_upgrade_trigger = {
		has_global_flag = palk_strait_cyclone_happened
	}

	keep_trigger = {
	}

great_wall_1 = {
	start = 6783 #Jizhou
	date = 1368.01.01 #Early Ming/from base game
	time = { months = 0	}
	build_cost = 0
	can_be_moved = no
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 1
	starting_tier = 2 #0
	type = monument

	build_trigger = {
		culture_group = east_asian
		OR = {
			has_owner_culture = yes
			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
		}
	}

	on_built = {
		show_ambient_object = the_great_wall_of_china
	}

	on_destroyed = {
		hide_ambient_object = the_great_wall_of_china
	}

	can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
		culture_group = east_asian
		OR = {
			has_owner_culture = yes
			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
		}
	}

	can_upgrade_trigger = {
		culture_group = east_asian
		OR = {
			has_owner_culture = yes
			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
		}
	}

	keep_trigger = {
	}

	tier_0 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 0
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 0
		}
		province_modifiers = {
		}
		area_modifier = {
		}
		country_modifiers = {
		}
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_1 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 120
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		province_modifiers = {
			#garrison_growth = 0.1
			local_hostile_attrition = 0.5
			local_defensiveness = 0.25
			local_garrison_size = 0.25
			local_fort_maintenance_modifier = 0.25
		}
		area_modifier = {
			#local_hostile_movement_speed = -0.1
		}
		country_modifiers = {
		}
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_2 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 240
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 2500
		}
		province_modifiers = {
			#garrison_growth = 0.2
			local_hostile_attrition = 0.5
			local_defensiveness = 0.35
			local_garrison_size = 0.35
			local_fort_maintenance_modifier = 0.35
		}
		area_modifier = {
			#local_hostile_movement_speed = -0.15
		}
		country_modifiers = {
		}
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_3 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 480
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 5000
		}
		province_modifiers = {
			#garrison_growth = 0.3
			local_hostile_attrition = 1
			local_defensiveness = 0.5
			local_garrison_size = 0.5
			local_fort_maintenance_modifier = 0.5
		}
		area_modifier = {
			#local_hostile_movement_speed = -0.2
		}
		country_modifiers = {
		}
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}
}

			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
		}
	}

		show_ambient_object = the_great_wall_of_china
	}

			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes

			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes

great_wall_4 = { #great_wall_8
	start = 6793 #Shanxi #Baodezhou / Piantou Pass
	date = 1368.01.01 #Early Ming/from base game
	time = { months = 0	}
	build_cost = 0
	can_be_moved = no
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 1
	starting_tier = 1 #0
	type = monument

	build_trigger = {
		culture_group = east_asian
		OR = {
			has_owner_culture = yes
			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
		}
	}

	on_built = {
		show_ambient_object = the_great_wall_of_china
	}

	on_destroyed = {
		hide_ambient_object = the_great_wall_of_china
	}

	can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
		culture_group = east_asian
		OR = {
			has_owner_culture = yes
			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
		}
	}

	can_upgrade_trigger = {
		culture_group = east_asian
		OR = {
			has_owner_culture = yes
			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
		}
	}

	keep_trigger = {
	}

	tier_0 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 0
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 0
		}
		province_modifiers = {
		}
		area_modifier = {
		}
		country_modifiers = {
		}
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_1 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 120
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		province_modifiers = {
			#garrison_growth = 0.1
			local_hostile_attrition = 0.5
			local_defensiveness = 0.25
			local_garrison_size = 0.25
			local_fort_maintenance_modifier = 0.25
		}
		area_modifier = {
			#local_hostile_movement_speed = -0.1
		}
		country_modifiers = {
		}
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_2 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 240
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 2500
		}
		province_modifiers = {
			#garrison_growth = 0.2
			local_hostile_attrition = 0.5
			local_defensiveness = 0.35
			local_garrison_size = 0.35
			local_fort_maintenance_modifier = 0.35
		}
		area_modifier = {
			#local_hostile_movement_speed = -0.15
		}
		country_modifiers = {
		}
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_3 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 480
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 5000
		}
		province_modifiers = {
			#garrison_growth = 0.3
			local_hostile_attrition = 1
			local_defensiveness = 0.5
			local_garrison_size = 0.5
			local_fort_maintenance_modifier = 0.5
		}
		area_modifier = {
			#local_hostile_movement_speed = -0.2
		}
		country_modifiers = {
		}
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
		}
	}

	can_upgrade_trigger = {
		culture_group = east_asian
		OR = {
			has_owner_culture = yes
			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
		}
	}

	keep_trigger = {
	}

	tier_0 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 0
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 0
		}
		province_modifiers = {
		}
		area_modifier = {
		}
		country_modifiers = {
		}
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_1 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 120
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		province_modifiers = {
			#garrison_growth = 0.1
			local_hostile_attrition = 0.5
			local_defensiveness = 0.25
			local_garrison_size = 0.25
			local_fort_maintenance_modifier = 0.25
		}
		area_modifier = {
			#local_hostile_movement_speed = -0.1
		}
		country_modifiers = {
		}
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_2 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 240
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 2500
		}
		province_modifiers = {
			#garrison_growth = 0.2
			local_hostile_attrition = 0.5
			local_defensiveness = 0.35
			local_garrison_size = 0.35
			local_fort_maintenance_modifier = 0.35
		}
		area_modifier = {
			#local_hostile_movement_speed = -0.15
		}
		country_modifiers = {
		}
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_3 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 480
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 5000
		}
		province_modifiers = {
			#garrison_growth = 0.3
			local_hostile_attrition = 1
			local_defensiveness = 0.5
			local_garrison_size = 0.5
			local_fort_maintenance_modifier = 0.5
		}
		area_modifier = {
			#local_hostile_movement_speed = -0.2
		}
		country_modifiers = {
		}
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}
}

great_wall_8 = { #great_wall_17
	start = 6835 #Ganzhou / Gansu
	date = 1368.01.01 #Early Ming/from base game
	time = { months = 0	}
	build_cost = 0
	can_be_moved = no
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 1
	starting_tier = 1 #0
	type = monument

	build_trigger = {
		culture_group = east_asian
		OR = {
			has_owner_culture = yes
			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
		}
	}

	on_built = {
		show_ambient_object = the_great_wall_of_china
	}

	on_destroyed = {
		hide_ambient_object = the_great_wall_of_china
	}

	can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
		culture_group = east_asian
		OR = {
			has_owner_culture = yes
			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
		}
	}

	can_upgrade_trigger = {
		culture_group = east_asian
		OR = {
			has_owner_culture = yes
			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
		}
	}

	keep_trigger = {
	}

	tier_0 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 0
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 0
		}
		province_modifiers = {
		}
		area_modifier = {
		}
		country_modifiers = {
		}
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_1 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 120
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		province_modifiers = {
			#garrison_growth = 0.1
			local_hostile_attrition = 0.5
			local_defensiveness = 0.25
			local_garrison_size = 0.25
			local_fort_maintenance_modifier = 0.25
		}
		area_modifier = {
			#local_hostile_movement_speed = -0.1
		}
		country_modifiers = {
		}
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_2 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 240
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 2500
		}
		province_modifiers = {
			#garrison_growth = 0.2
			local_hostile_attrition = 0.5
			local_defensiveness = 0.35
			local_garrison_size = 0.35
			local_fort_maintenance_modifier = 0.35
		}
		area_modifier = {
			#local_hostile_movement_speed = -0.15
		}
		country_modifiers = {
		}
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_3 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 480
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 5000
		}
		province_modifiers = {
			#garrison_growth = 0.3
			local_hostile_attrition = 1
			local_defensiveness = 0.5
			local_garrison_size = 0.5
			local_fort_maintenance_modifier = 0.5
		}
		area_modifier = {
			#local_hostile_movement_speed = -0.2
		}
		country_modifiers = {
		}
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}
}
